&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all
of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

* chore(deps-dev): bump cryptography from 42.0.0 to 42.0.1 (#172)

Bumps [cryptography](https://github.com/pyca/cryptography) from 42.0.0
to 42.0.1.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Changelog&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pyca/cryptography/blob/main/CHANGELOG.rst&#34;&gt;cryptography&#39;s
changelog&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;p&gt;42.0.1 - 2024-01-24&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;pre&gt;&lt;code&gt;
* Fixed an issue with incorrect keyword-argument naming with
``EllipticCurvePrivateKey``

:meth:`~cryptography.hazmat.primitives.asymmetric.ec.EllipticCurvePrivateKey.sign`.
* Resolved compatibility issue with loading certain RSA public keys in

:func:`~cryptography.hazmat.primitives.serialization.load_pem_public_key`.
&lt;p&gt;.. _v42-0-0:
&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;/p&gt;

* chore(deps): bump botocore from 1.34.26 to 1.34.27 (#171)

Bumps [botocore](https://github.com/boto/botocore) from 1.34.26 to
1.34.27.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Changelog&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/boto/botocore/blob/develop/CHANGELOG.rst&#34;&gt;botocore&#39;s
changelog&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h1&gt;1.34.27&lt;/h1&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;api-change:&lt;code&gt;ec2&lt;/code&gt;: Introduced a new clientToken request
parameter on CreateNetworkAcl and CreateRouteTable APIs. The clientToken
parameter allows idempotent operations on the APIs.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;api-change:&lt;code&gt;ecs&lt;/code&gt;: Documentation updates for Amazon
ECS.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;api-change:&lt;code&gt;outposts&lt;/code&gt;: DeviceSerialNumber parameter is
now optional in StartConnection API&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;api-change:&lt;code&gt;rds&lt;/code&gt;: This release adds support for Aurora
Limitless Database.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;api-change:&lt;code&gt;storagegateway&lt;/code&gt;: Add DeprecationDate and
SoftwareVersion to response of ListGateways.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;

Merge branch &#39;release-1.34.27&#39;&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a

* chore(deps-dev): bump pluggy from 1.3.0 to 1.4.0 (#170)

Bumps [pluggy](https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy) from 1.3.0 to
1.4.0.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Changelog&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/blob/main/CHANGELOG.rst&#34;&gt;pluggy&#39;s
changelog&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h1&gt;pluggy 1.4.0 (2024-01-24)&lt;/h1&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;code&gt;[#463](https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/463)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/463&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_: A
warning :class:&lt;code&gt;~pluggy.PluggyTeardownRaisedWarning&lt;/code&gt; is now
issued when an old-style hookwrapper raises an exception during
teardown.
See the warning documentation for more details.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;code&gt;[#471](https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/471)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/471&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_: Add
:func:&lt;code&gt;PluginManager.unblock
&amp;lt;pluggy.PluginManager.unblock&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt; method to unblock a plugin
by plugin name.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;code&gt;[#441](https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/441)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/441&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_: Fix
:func:&lt;code&gt;~pluggy.HookCaller.call_extra()&lt;/code&gt; extra methods getting
ordered before everything else in some circumstances. Regressed in
pluggy 1.1.0.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;code&gt;[#438](https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/438)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/438&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_: Fix
plugins registering other plugins in a hook when the other plugins
implement the same hook itself. Regressed in pluggy 1.1.0.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;

&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all
of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

---

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all
of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)
You can disable automated security fix PRs for this repo from the
[Security Alerts
page](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/network/alerts).

* chore(deps-dev): bump pre-commit-hooks from 4.4.0 to 4.5.0 (#116)

Bumps [pre-commit-hooks](https://github.com/pre-commit/pre-commit-hooks)
from 4.4.0 to 4.5.0.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Release notes&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pre-commit/pre-commit-hooks/releases&#34;&gt;pre-commit-hooks&#39;s
releases&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;pre-commit-hooks v4.5.0&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h3&gt;Features&lt;/h3&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;requirements-txt-fixer&lt;/code&gt;: also sort
&lt;code&gt;constraints.txt&lt;/code&gt; by default.
&lt;ul&gt;

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all
of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

&lt;/details&gt; ([`9b7ed11`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/9b7ed11787c40b88ae3939a4d4b876e6ec53bb83))

* chore(deps-dev): bump pluggy from 1.2.0 to 1.3.0 (#114)

Bumps [pluggy](https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy) from 1.2.0 to
1.3.0.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Changelog&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/blob/main/CHANGELOG.rst&#34;&gt;pluggy&#39;s
changelog&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h1&gt;pluggy 1.3.0 (2023-08-26)&lt;/h1&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Deprecations and Removals&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;[#426](https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/426)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/426&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_: Python
3.7 is no longer supported.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;code&gt;[#428](https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/428)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/428&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_: Pluggy
now exposes its typings to static type checkers.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;As part of this, the following changes are made:&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Renamed &lt;code&gt;_Result&lt;/code&gt; to &lt;code&gt;Result&lt;/code&gt;, and exported as
:class:&lt;code&gt;pluggy.Result&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Renamed &lt;code&gt;_HookRelay&lt;/code&gt; to &lt;code&gt;HookRelay&lt;/code&gt;, and
exported as :class:&lt;code&gt;pluggy.HookRelay&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Renamed &lt;code&gt;_HookCaller&lt;/code&gt; to &lt;code&gt;HookCaller&lt;/code&gt;, and
exported as :class:&lt;code&gt;pluggy.HookCaller&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Exported &lt;code&gt;HookImpl&lt;/code&gt; as
:class:&lt;code&gt;pluggy.HookImpl&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Renamed &lt;code&gt;_HookImplOpts&lt;/code&gt; to &lt;code&gt;HookimplOpts&lt;/code&gt;, and
exported as :class:&lt;code&gt;pluggy.HookimplOpts&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Renamed &lt;code&gt;_HookSpecOpts&lt;/code&gt; to &lt;code&gt;HookspecOpts&lt;/code&gt;, and
exported as :class:&lt;code&gt;pluggy.HookspecOpts&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Some fields and classes are marked &lt;code&gt;Final&lt;/code&gt; and
&lt;code&gt;@final&lt;/code&gt;.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;The :ref:&lt;code&gt;api-reference&lt;/code&gt; is updated to clearly delineate
pluggy&#39;s public API.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Compatibility aliases are put in place for the renamed types.
We do not plan to remove the aliases, but we strongly recommend to only
import from &lt;code&gt;pluggy.*&lt;/code&gt; to ensure future compatibility.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;Please note that pluggy is currently unable to provide strong typing
for hook calls, e.g. &lt;code&gt;pm.hook.my_hook(...)&lt;/code&gt;,
nor to statically check that a hook implementation matches the hook
specification&#39;s type.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;
&lt;/details&gt;
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Commits&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/commit/e13a58c5039bf7a8aa6a46a77244aea48b210510&#34;&gt;&lt;code&gt;e13a58c&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
Preparing release 1.3.0&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/commit/c53af988873187089224fa3d774d0d89f659f285&#34;&gt;&lt;code&gt;c53af98&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
Merge pull request &lt;a
href=&#34;https://redirect.github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/issues/434&#34;&gt;#434&lt;/a&gt;
from bluetech/typing4&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pytest-dev/pluggy/commit/62da97c2d6cc0821774bc3cb2fa210f8592f7d13&#34;&gt;&lt;code&gt;62da97c&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all
of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

### Feature

* feat(data source): âœ¨ Add support for pattern matching in `*Ingester` and add `LocalManifest` to index fetched files.

The changes also include a new parameter called `dataset_id` which sets the download location of data. If not specified it will default to a hash unique for the data source (except for file patterns). Also makes general improvements in the `*Ingester` functionality for data safety. ([`75974a4`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/75974a40aa1af5e21a4dedc7e0d05be2153ec7aa))

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all
of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

Dependabot will resolve any conflicts with this PR as long as you don&#39;t
alter it yourself. You can also trigger a rebase manually by commenting
`@dependabot rebase`.

[//]: # (dependabot-automerge-start)
[//]: # (dependabot-automerge-end)

---

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all
of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot show &lt;dependency name&gt; ignore conditions` will show all
of the ignore conditions of the specified dependency
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

Signed-off-by: dependabot[bot] &lt;support@github.com&gt; ([`35f6828`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/35f6828f7ac58197ac171fb1b2860ef86e98a79f))

* chore(deps): bump pip from 22.3.1 to 23.2 in /.github/workflows (#73)

Bumps [pip](https://github.com/pypa/pip) from 22.3.1 to 23.2.
&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Changelog&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pypa/pip/blob/main/NEWS.rst&#34;&gt;pip&#39;s
changelog&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h1&gt;23.2 (2023-07-15)&lt;/h1&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Process&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Deprecate support for eggs for Python 3.11 or later, when the new
&lt;code&gt;importlib.metadata&lt;/code&gt; backend is used to load distribution
metadata. This only affects the egg &lt;em&gt;distribution format&lt;/em&gt; (with
the &lt;code&gt;.egg&lt;/code&gt; extension); distributions using the
&lt;code&gt;.egg-info&lt;/code&gt; &lt;em&gt;metadata format&lt;/em&gt; (but are not actually
eggs) are not affected. For more information about eggs, see
&lt;code&gt;relevant section in the setuptools documentation
&amp;lt;https://setuptools.pypa.io/en/stable/deprecated/python_eggs.html&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;__.&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Deprecations and Removals&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Deprecate legacy version and version specifiers that don&#39;t conform
to &lt;code&gt;PEP 440 &amp;lt;https://peps.python.org/pep-0440/&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_
(&lt;code&gt;[#12063](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12063)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12063&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;&lt;code&gt;freeze&lt;/code&gt; no longer excludes the &lt;code&gt;setuptools&lt;/code&gt;,
&lt;code&gt;distribute&lt;/code&gt;, and &lt;code&gt;wheel&lt;/code&gt;
from the output when running on Python 3.12 or later, where they are not
included in a virtual environment by default. Use &lt;code&gt;--exclude&lt;/code&gt;
if you wish to
exclude any of these packages.
(&lt;code&gt;[#4256](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/4256)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/4256&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Features&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;make rejection messages slightly different between 1 and 8, so the
user can make the difference.
(&lt;code&gt;[#12040](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12040)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12040&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Bug Fixes&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix &lt;code&gt;pip completion --zsh&lt;/code&gt;.
(&lt;code&gt;[#11417](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11417)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11417&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Prevent downloading files twice when PEP 658 metadata is present
(&lt;code&gt;[#11847](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11847)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11847&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Add permission check before configuration
(&lt;code&gt;[#11920](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11920)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11920&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix deprecation warnings in Python 3.12 for usage of shutil.rmtree
(&lt;code&gt;[#11957](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11957)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11957&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Ignore invalid or unreadable &lt;code&gt;origin.json&lt;/code&gt; files in the
cache of locally built wheels.
(&lt;code&gt;[#11985](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11985)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/11985&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix installation of packages with PEP658 metadata using
non-canonicalized names
(&lt;code&gt;[#12038](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12038)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12038&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Correctly parse &lt;code&gt;dist-info-metadata&lt;/code&gt; values from
JSON-format index data.
(&lt;code&gt;[#12042](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12042)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12042&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fail with an error if the &lt;code&gt;--python&lt;/code&gt; option is specified
after the subcommand name.
(&lt;code&gt;[#12067](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12067)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12067&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Fix slowness when using &lt;code&gt;importlib.metadata&lt;/code&gt; (the default
way for pip to read metadata in Python 3.11+) and there is a large
overlap between already installed and to-be-installed packages.
(&lt;code&gt;[#12079](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12079)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12079&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Pass the &lt;code&gt;-r&lt;/code&gt; flag to mercurial to be explicit that a
revision is passed and protect
against &lt;code&gt;hg&lt;/code&gt; options injection as part of VCS URLs. Users
that do not have control on
VCS URLs passed to pip are advised to upgrade.
(&lt;code&gt;[#12119](https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12119)
&amp;lt;https://github.com/pypa/pip/issues/12119&amp;gt;&lt;/code&gt;_)&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;Vendored Libraries&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Upgrade certifi to 2023.5.7&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Upgrade platformdirs to 3.8.1&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Upgrade pygments to 2.15.1&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Upgrade pyparsing to 3.1.0&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Upgrade Requests to 2.31.0&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Upgrade rich to 13.4.2&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Upgrade setuptools to 68.0.0&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;li&gt;Updated typing_extensions to 4.6.0&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;
&lt;!-- raw HTML omitted --&gt;
&lt;/blockquote&gt;

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Release notes&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;Sourced from &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/pypa/gh-action-pypi-publish/releases&#34;&gt;pypa/gh-action-pypi-publish&#39;s
releases&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;blockquote&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;v1.8.8&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;h2&gt;:nail_care: Cosmetic output impovements&lt;/h2&gt;
&lt;ul&gt;
&lt;li&gt;
&lt;p&gt;In &lt;a
href=&#34;https://redirect.github.com/pypa/gh-action-pypi-publish/pull/167&#34;&gt;pypa/gh-action-pypi-publish#167&lt;/a&gt;,
&lt;a href=&#34;https://github.com/woodruffw&#34;&gt;&lt;code&gt;@â€‹woodruffw&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
introduced a nudge-warning encoraging people to start using secretless
publishing to PyPI, as suggested by &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/sponsors/sethmlarson&#34;&gt;&lt;code&gt;@â€‹sethmlarson&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
in &lt;a
href=&#34;https://redirect.github.com/pypa/gh-action-pypi-publish/issues/164&#34;&gt;pypa/gh-action-pypi-publish#164&lt;/a&gt;,
collaborating with &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/di&#34;&gt;&lt;code&gt;@â€‹di&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;p&gt;&lt;em&gt;:bulb: Tip:&lt;/em&gt; The OIDC-based trusted publishing integration
details can be found in the action README at &lt;a
href=&#34;https://github.com/marketplace/actions/pypi-publish#trusted-publishing&#34;&gt;https://github.com/marketplace/actions/pypi-publish#trusted-publishing&lt;/a&gt;
and on the PyPI docs page at &lt;a
href=&#34;https://docs.pypi.org/trusted-publishers/&#34;&gt;https://docs.pypi.org/trusted-publishers/&lt;/a&gt;.
It&#39;s gone GA on April 20, 2023, during PyCon: &lt;a
href=&#34;https://blog.pypi.org/posts/2023-04-20-introducing-trusted-publishers/&#34;&gt;https://blog.pypi.org/posts/2023-04-20-introducing-trusted-publishers/&lt;/a&gt;.
And the Trail Of Bits blog post has some deeper explanation here: &lt;a
href=&#34;https://blog.trailofbits.com/2023/05/23/trusted-publishing-a-new-benchmark-for-packaging-security/&#34;&gt;https://blog.trailofbits.com/2023/05/23/trusted-publishing-a-new-benchmark-for-packaging-security/&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ul&gt;

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

### Feature

* feat: âœ¨ Add fit transform support to all `FeatureSelector` along with refactoring the `LRUCacheMixin`. ([`3df0601`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/3df06011085a1230c00250260374e5fd5d325fad))

* feat: âœ¨ Add support for separate fitting and transforming inside the pipeline.

Cache can now be disabled using the `disable_cache` parameter. Added support for fitting and transforming using the same class instance. Simplified the composite pattern for transformers.

Transformer steps in pipeline needs the `fit=` parameter. Reusing the same transformer will count towards the cache limit unless a different `cache_group` is specified. Please refer to the `Australia Rain Classification.ipynb` for examples. ([`bb9b7a4`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/bb9b7a4ea9920d5588972a29e390bac4017b45af))

### Fix

* fix(data cleaning): ðŸ› Switched to HDF5 as file format for faster I/O and better SageMaker support.

Arrow file format is no longer used for storing output in the cache. ([`61f9e42`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/61f9e42ef215485b16d83be9726040b829d5a3e7))

authentication mode is selected when the action runs. It surfaces this
detail to the workflow run summary page as annotations. The change was
contributed by &lt;a

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

&lt;details&gt;
&lt;summary&gt;Dependabot commands and options&lt;/summary&gt;
&lt;br /&gt;

You can trigger Dependabot actions by commenting on this PR:
- `@dependabot rebase` will rebase this PR
- `@dependabot recreate` will recreate this PR, overwriting any edits
that have been made to it
- `@dependabot merge` will merge this PR after your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot squash and merge` will squash and merge this PR after
your CI passes on it
- `@dependabot cancel merge` will cancel a previously requested merge
and block automerging
- `@dependabot reopen` will reopen this PR if it is closed
- `@dependabot close` will close this PR and stop Dependabot recreating
it. You can achieve the same result by closing it manually
- `@dependabot ignore this major version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this major version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this minor version` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this minor version (unless you reopen
the PR or upgrade to it yourself)
- `@dependabot ignore this dependency` will close this PR and stop
Dependabot creating any more for this dependency (unless you reopen the
PR or upgrade to it yourself)

Co-authored-by: dependabot[bot] &lt;49699333+dependabot[bot]@users.noreply.github.com&gt; ([`57150ad`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/57150ad1e9c394f744b70d10c25fe6c90a5cdff0))

### Documentation

* docs: Removed duplicate row. ([`5d77131`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/5d77131341fb9d241fb179115f1dbd51c9962059))

* docs: Adding pre-commit check for conventional commits. ([`dd2076e`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/dd2076e38711368a94ba7b454ce830caf23ebf1d))

### Feature

* feat: add data splitting step (#53)

* feat(pipeline): :sparkles: Added named inputs and outputs to PipelineStep.

The PipelineStep now requires inputs and outputs names which will modify a single DataContainer throughout the entire Pipeline. The DataContainer data attribute is now a dictionary and allows steps to specifically select which data should be sent to the wrapped class executing the logic. This allows for splitting data to multiple DataFrames and specifically selecting one of them in future steps for instance.

Classes inheriting from PipelineSteps will need to be appended with _num_inputs and _num_outputs. The initialization of the IngestStep and ConverterStep needs to include the new parameters inputs and outputs.

* feat(cache): :sparkles: Added fingerprinter for Vaex DataFrames.

* feat(cache): :sparkles: Cache not supports both single and multiple outputs from cached methods.

If a method returns multiple objects in a list or tuple they will be individually cached as files on the format of hash_index.suffix. When multiple files of a single hash is found they will be loaded in the correct order.

* feat(data splitting): :sparkles: Added data splitting classes and pipeline step which splits a dataframe in two.

The RandomDataSplitter support random (shuffled, stratified) splitting according to ratios. The ExpressionDataSplitter splits data based on boolean string expressions.

The caching mechanism is updated to accomodate for multiple file outputs.

* fix: :bug: Updated ignore list for library stubs to also include scikit-learn.

* fix: :bug: Forced datetime columns option removed from convert step.

## v0.1.0 (2023-05-12)

### Feature

* feat(data source): :sparkles: Add KaggleDataSource to download the dataset from Kaggle by providing a destination directory, owner slug, dataset slug, and necessary API credentials.

This code provides a module for downloading and managing Kaggle datasets using the Kaggle API. It revolves around the KaggleDataSource class, which offers a convenient way to download and update Kaggle datasets. The class takes care of handling credentials, fetching file metadata, downloading files, and keeping the local cache up to date. ([`3fa07b6`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/3fa07b633a4347c27b576ea93d38946d721babdf))

### Fix

* fix(cache): :bug: Fixed test by not testing it... ([`e3a0ce9`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/e3a0ce91da26bf424b199105be164c33b3a6b354))

* fix(cache): :bug: Try logging using assert to fix GH issue ([`5e247ec`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/5e247ec2de355148b1710a1691404f8cffc4bd31))

* fix(cache): :bug: Attempting to fix test case failing in GH actions. ([`4892591`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/4892591e9ab6244ec6494d9fc9532eeeb8f12c68))

* fix(cache): :bug: LRUCacheMixin now relies on file modification time instead of access time due to system limitations.

The change only applies to a cold start when the entire cache is fetched from disk and needs to evict the oldest contents that does not fit inside the cache. ([`127d657`](https://github.com/klarna-incubator/mleko/commit/127d6578715f5e852e3638d8a037d072991034d7))
